## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x0001 [0x20] SET_CLI_EVENT_UC_FLAG: Lock player control
  1: 0x0003 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[0] = 0*
  2: 0x0008 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[1] = 0*
  3: 0x000D [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[2] = 0*
```
